NEXT:
  current progress
  - The environment setup plan is thoroughly adjusted for CPU-only operation, excluding all GPU/NVIDIA-specific instructions, containers, and tests.
  - The Dockerfile is based on ubuntu:22.04, installs extensive system dependencies, sets up locale, attempts to install a user-specified Python version (default 3.12) via deadsnakes PPA, and configures Jupyter, AWS CLI, s3cmd, and TAO Tutorials repo.
  - The Docker build failed at the step adding the deadsnakes PPA and installing Python 3.12, indicating a problem with the repository or package installation on Ubuntu 22.04.
  - All other steps in the Dockerfile are not executed due to this failure.
  - The plan and Dockerfile are consistent with CPU-only mode, but Python version installation is the blocking issue.
  next step
  - Investigate and resolve the Python installation failure on Ubuntu 22.04:
    - The deadsnakes PPA is generally unnecessary for Python >=3.10 on Ubuntu 22.04, as python3.10, python3.11, and python3.12 are available via official repositories.
    - Remove the line `RUN add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && apt-get update && ...` and instead use:
      ```
      RUN apt-get update && \
          apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
          ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
          rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
      ```
    - Confirm that `${PYTHON_VERSION}` is set to 3.12 or 3.11, both supported by Ubuntu 22.04.
  - Rebuild the Docker image after this change and verify successful installation of the desired Python version.
  - If build is successful, proceed with later steps: pip upgrades, Python package installations, and project setup as per the plan.

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Set noninteractive for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Allow overriding Python version at build time
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Install the desired Python version via deadsnakes if not already default
  RUN add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Upgrade pip to >21.06 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python${PYTHON_VERSION} && \
      python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Make sure pip3 is also updated (for compatibility)
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Install Jupyter and notebook runtime dependencies (requirements.txt and requirements-pip.txt will be installed later)
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  # Install AWS CLI and s3cmd
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  # Clone the TAO Tutorials repository if not already present
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  # Copy project to /workspace for a clean working directory, allow for host mounts
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Install Python requirements (requirements.txt in project root or notebooks/)
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  # Install additional notebook/TAO Launcher dependencies if present
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  # Make sure /workspace is writable
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  # Set environment variables for CPU-only operation
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  # Expose common ports for Jupyter, NGINX, SeaweedFS, MongoDB
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Set noninteractive for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Allow overriding Python version at build time
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Install the desired Python version via official Ubuntu repository
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Upgrade pip to >21.06 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python${PYTHON_VERSION} && \
      python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Make sure pip3 is also updated (for compatibility)
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Install Jupyter and notebook runtime dependencies (requirements.txt and requirements-pip.txt will be installed later)
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  # Install AWS CLI and s3cmd
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  # Clone the TAO Tutorials repository if not already present
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  # Copy project to /workspace for a clean working directory, allow for host mounts
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Install Python requirements (requirements.txt in project root or notebooks/)
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  # Install additional notebook/TAO Launcher dependencies if present
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  # Make sure /workspace is writable
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  # Set environment variables for CPU-only operation
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  # Expose common ports for Jupyter, NGINX, SeaweedFS, MongoDB
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Set noninteractive for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Allow overriding Python version at build time
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for newer Python versions
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common && \
      add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa -y && \
      apt-get update
  # Install the desired Python version via deadsnakes PPA
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Upgrade pip to >21.06 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python${PYTHON_VERSION} && \
      python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Make sure pip3 is also updated (for compatibility)
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Install Jupyter and notebook runtime dependencies (requirements.txt and requirements-pip.txt will be installed later)
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  # Install AWS CLI and s3cmd
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  # Clone the TAO Tutorials repository if not already present
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  # Copy project to /workspace for a clean working directory, allow for host mounts
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Install Python requirements (requirements.txt in project root or notebooks/)
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  # Install additional notebook/TAO Launcher dependencies if present
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  # Make sure /workspace is writable
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  # Set environment variables for CPU-only operation
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  # Expose common ports for Jupyter, NGINX, SeaweedFS, MongoDB
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Set noninteractive for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Allow overriding Python version at build time
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Install the desired Python version directly (no PPA required for Ubuntu 22.04)
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Upgrade pip to >21.06 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python${PYTHON_VERSION} && \
      python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Make sure pip3 is also updated (for compatibility)
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  # Install Jupyter and notebook runtime dependencies (requirements.txt and requirements-pip.txt will be installed later)
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  # Install AWS CLI and s3cmd
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  # Clone the TAO Tutorials repository if not already present
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  # Copy project to /workspace for a clean working directory, allow for host mounts
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Install Python requirements (requirements.txt in project root or notebooks/)
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  # Install additional notebook/TAO Launcher dependencies if present
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  # Make sure /workspace is writable
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  # Set environment variables for CPU-only operation
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  # Expose common ports for Jupyter, NGINX, SeaweedFS, MongoDB
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for newer Python versions if needed
  RUN add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && apt-get update
  # Install the desired Python version
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Upgrade pip to >21.06 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python${PYTHON_VERSION} && \
      python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Install the desired Python version directly from Ubuntu repositories
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends python${PYTHON_VERSION} python${PYTHON_VERSION}-dev python${PYTHON_VERSION}-distutils python${PYTHON_VERSION}-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python${PYTHON_VERSION} /usr/bin/python3 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Upgrade pip to >21.06 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python${PYTHON_VERSION} && \
      python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  RUN python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python${PYTHON_VERSION} -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG PYTHON_VERSION=3.12
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=${PYTHON_VERSION}
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        rsync \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.12
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends software-properties-common && \
      add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        python3.12 \
        python3.12-dev \
        python3.12-distutils \
        python3.12-venv && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.12 /usr/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.12 /usr/local/bin/python && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Upgrade pip to >21.1 for chosen Python version
  RUN curl -sS https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py | python3.12 && \
      python3.12 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  RUN python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python3.12 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Install basic utilities and system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        software-properties-common \
        apt-transport-https \
        ca-certificates \
        wget \
        curl \
        git \
        tar \
        unzip \
        gzip \
        rsync \
        openssh-client \
        jq \
        postgresql-client \
        nginx \
        build-essential \
        libssl-dev \
        libffi-dev \
        libpq-dev \
        libxml2-dev \
        libxslt1-dev \
        zlib1g-dev \
        libbz2-dev \
        libreadline-dev \
        libsqlite3-dev \
        libncursesw5-dev \
        libgdbm-dev \
        liblzma-dev \
        tk-dev \
        libcurl4-openssl-dev \
        libfreetype6-dev \
        pkg-config \
        locales \
        vim \
        nano \
        net-tools \
        iputils-ping \
        openssl \
        ssh \
        lsof \
        sudo \
        less \
        python3-distutils \
        python3-venv \
        python3-pip \
        && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Use Ubuntu native Python 3.10 for 22.04
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.10 /usr/bin/python3 && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.10 /usr/local/bin/python
  # Ensure locale is set (for Python and Jupyter)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade "pip>=21.1"
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir \
        notebook \
        jupyterlab \
        ipykernel \
        ipywidgets \
        jupyter_contrib_nbextensions \
        jupyterthemes \
        requests
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir awscli s3cmd
  WORKDIR /tmp
  RUN git clone https://github.com/NVIDIA/tao_tutorials.git /opt/tao_tutorials
  RUN mkdir -p /workspace && cp -r /opt/tao_tutorials/. /workspace/
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt; fi
  RUN if [ -f notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt ]; then python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir -r notebooks/tao_launcher_starter_kit/deps/requirements-pip.txt; fi
  RUN chmod -R a+rwX /workspace
  ENV TAO_CPU_MODE=true
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  ENV PIP_DISABLE_PIP_VERSION_CHECK=1
  ENV PIP_NO_CACHE_DIR=1
  EXPOSE 8888 8090 8443 27017 9333 8333 8080
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
